	effect = {}

giga_menu_prev = {
	potential = { exists = from }
	allow = { always = yes }
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			from = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_00 }
					remove_country_flag = giga_menu_page_00
					set_country_flag = giga_menu_page_03
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_presets }
					remove_country_flag = giga_menu_page_presets
					set_country_flag = giga_menu_page_00
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_presets_02 }
					remove_country_flag = giga_menu_page_presets_02
					set_country_flag = giga_menu_page_presets
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_01 }
					remove_country_flag = giga_menu_page_01
					set_country_flag = giga_menu_page_presets_02
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_02 }
					remove_country_flag = giga_menu_page_02
					set_country_flag = giga_menu_page_01
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_03 }
					remove_country_flag = giga_menu_page_03
					set_country_flag = giga_menu_page_02
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

giga_menu_next = {
	potential = { exists = from }
	allow = { always = yes }
	effect = {
		hidden_effect = {
			from = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_00 }
					remove_country_flag = giga_menu_page_00
					set_country_flag = giga_menu_page_presets
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_presets }
					remove_country_flag = giga_menu_page_presets
					set_country_flag = giga_menu_page_presets_02
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_presets_02 }
					remove_country_flag = giga_menu_page_presets_02
					set_country_flag = giga_menu_page_01
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_01 }
					remove_country_flag = giga_menu_page_01
					set_country_flag = giga_menu_page_02
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_02 }
					remove_country_flag = giga_menu_page_02
					set_country_flag = giga_menu_page_03
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_03 }
					remove_country_flag = giga_menu_page_03
					set_country_flag = giga_menu_page_00
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

giga_presets_random = {
	potential = { exists = from from = { has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_presets } }
	allow = { custom_tooltip = { fail_text = "must_not_have_started_game" NOT = { has_global_flag = giga_game_started } } }
	effect = { hidden_effect = { from = { giga_preset_random = yes } } }
}

giga_fe_megas_disabled = {
	potential = {
		exists = from
		from = {
			has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_00
			has_global_flag = giga_fe_megas_disabled

		}

		set_global_flag = giga_core_aeternum_3
	}

giga_habitat_disabled = {
	potential = {
		exists = from
		from = {
			has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_01
			has_global_flag = giga_habitats_disabled
		}
	}
	allow = { always = yes }
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "giga_menu_enabled"
		remove_global_flag = giga_habitats_disabled
	}
}

giga_habitat_enabled = {
	potential = {
		exists = from
		from = {
			has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_01
			NOT = { has_global_flag = giga_habitats_disabled }
		}
	}
	allow = { always = yes }
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "giga_menu_disabled"
		set_global_flag = giga_habitats_disabled
	}
}

giga_habitat_unlimited = {
	potential = {
		exists = from
		from = {
			has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_01
			has_global_flag = giga_habitats_unlimited
		}
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "must_not_have_started_game"
			NOT = { has_global_flag = giga_game_started }
		}
		hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = giga_habitats_disabled } }
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "giga_menu_u"
		remove_flags_habitats = yes
		set_global_flag = giga_habitats_pop
		set_global_flag = giga_habitats_pop_25
	}
}

giga_planetshipyard_u_disabled = { potential = { exists = from from = { has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_02 } OR = { has_global_flag = planetshipyard_disabled NOT = { has_global_flag = planetshipyard_capped_u } } }									allow = { custom_tooltip = { fail_text = "must_not_have_started_game" NOT = { has_global_flag = giga_game_started } } hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = planetshipyard_disabled } } }				effect = { remove_flags_planetshipyard = yes set_global_flag = planetshipyard_capped_u } }


giga_vr_disabled = {
	potential = {
		exists = from
		from = {
			has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_01
			has_global_flag = virtual_reality_disabled
		}
	}
	allow = { NOT = { has_global_flag = matrioshka_brain_disabled } }
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "giga_menu_enabled"
		remove_global_flag = virtual_reality_disabled
	}
}
giga_vr_enabled = {
	potential = {
		exists = from
		from = {
			has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_01
			NOT = { has_global_flag = virtual_reality_disabled }
		}
	}
	allow = { NOT = { has_global_flag = matrioshka_brain_disabled } }
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "giga_menu_disabled"
		set_global_flag = virtual_reality_disabled
		remove_global_flag = giga_virtual_industry
	}
}
giga_vr_base = {
	potential = {
		exists = from
		from = {
			has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_01
			NOT = { has_global_flag = giga_virtual_industry }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = virtual_reality_disabled }
		}
	}
	allow = { NOT = { has_global_flag = matrioshka_brain_disabled has_global_flag = giga_virtual_industry } }
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "giga_menu_virtual_reality_enabled"
		#set_global_flag = giga_virtual_industry
	}
}
giga_vr_base_disabled = {
	potential = {
		exists = from
		from = {
			has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_01
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = giga_virtual_industry
				has_global_flag = virtual_reality_disabled
			}
		}
	}
	allow = { NOT = { has_global_flag = matrioshka_brain_disabled } has_global_flag = giga_virtual_industry }
	effect = {
		remove_global_flag = giga_virtual_industry
	}
}

celestial_printing_x = { #now shows war moon printing as disabled if warmoons are disabled
	potential = {
		exists = from
		from = {
			has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_00
			has_global_flag = giga_celestial_printing_moon_disabled
		}
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = "must_not_have_started_game"
		hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = giga_game_started } }
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "giga_celestial_printing_disabled"
		hidden_effect = { remove_global_flag = giga_celestial_printing_moon_disabled remove_global_flag = warmoon_disabled }
	}
}

ruined_ships_divide_2 = {
	potential = {
		exists = from
		from = {
			has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_00
		}
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "must_not_have_started_game"
			hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = giga_game_started } }
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "giga_ruined_ships_divide_2"
		hidden_effect = { 
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				divide_variable = {
					which = giga_ruined_warships_perc
					value = 2
				}
				ceiling_variable = giga_ruined_warships_perc
			}
		}
	}
}

ruined_ships_subtract_1 = {
	potential = {
		exists = from
		from = {
			has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_00
		}
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "must_not_have_started_game"
			hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = giga_game_started } }
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "giga_ruined_ship_perc_low_enough"
			hidden_trigger = { 
				NOT = {
					event_target:global_event_country = {
						check_variable = {
							which = giga_ruined_warships_perc
							value < 10
						}
					}
				} 
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "giga_ruined_ships_subtract_1"
		hidden_effect = { 
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				subtract_variable = {
					which = giga_ruined_warships_perc
					value = 10
				}
				ceiling_variable = giga_ruined_warships_perc
			}
		}
	}
}

ruined_ships_reset = {
	potential = {
		exists = from
		from = {
			has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_00
		}
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = "must_not_have_started_game"
		hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = giga_game_started } }
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "giga_ruined_ships_reset"
		hidden_effect = { 
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				set_variable = {
					which = giga_ruined_warships_perc
					value = 100
				}
				ceiling_variable = giga_ruined_warships_perc
			}
		}
	}
}

ruined_ships_multiply_2 = {
	potential = {
		exists = from
		from = {
			has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_00
		}
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "must_not_have_started_game"
			hidden_trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = giga_game_started } }
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "giga_ruined_ship_perc_high_enough"
			hidden_trigger = { 
				NOT = {
					event_target:global_event_country = {
						check_variable = {
							which = giga_ruined_warships_perc
							value > 25000
						}
					}
				} 
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "giga_ruined_ships_multiply_2"
		hidden_effect = { 
			event_target:global_event_country = {
				multiply_variable = {
					which = giga_ruined_warships_perc
					value = 2
				}
				ceiling_variable = giga_ruined_warships_perc
			}
		}
	}
}

#Vintage or not
katzenartig_x_serious = {
	potential = {
		exists = from
		from = {
			has_country_flag = giga_menu_page_00
			NOR = {
				has_global_flag = silly_flusionian_portraits_enabled
				has_global_flag = silly_flusionian_portraits_enabled_cattail
			}
		}
	}
	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "must_not_have_started_game"
			NOT = { has_global_flag = giga_game_started }
		}
		hidden_trigger = {
			NOR = {
				has_global_flag = silly_flusionian_portraits_enabled
				has_global_flag = silly_flusionian_portraits_enabled_cattail
			}
		}
	}
	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = "giga_flusion_serious"
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = silly_flusionian_portraits_enabled_cattail }
			remove_global_flag = silly_flusionian_portraits_enabled_cattail
		}
		set_global_flag = silly_flusionian_portraits_enabled 
	}
}
